“Huh? Celestial Emperor Fairy, you also know about me building a large tomb for myself?” exclaimed Song Shuhang. “You’ve been spying on me?” The Celestial Thearch’s head throbbed.

She had recently been trying to adapt to Soft Feather’s erratic thought patterns, but whenever she interacted with this group of people whose thoughts jumped like cliffs, she still felt mentally exhausted.

When communicating with such individuals, one could never predict how they would respond or where they would steer the conversation.

What was even more awkward was... she had indeed spied on Song Shuhang before. Hence, she knew where Song Shuhangs main body and clone were, and whether they would hinder her ‘passing the throne’ grand plan.

However, if she were to respond with something like ‘l have spied on you’, she felt like she would be stooping down to Song Shuhangs level, doing the same thing as him.

So, the Celestial Thearch fell silent again, opting not to speak.

“As for the coffin, Senior White has already prepared a ‘flying sword style wooden coffin’ for me,” Song Shuhang replied. The flying sword coffin was trendy and cool, and most importantly, it was in the shape of a sword.

Although he had long given up on his talent in swordsmanship and admitted the fact that he was a macheteman, this did not stop him from admiring the flying sword.

“Do you think it’s as simple as a coffin? I’m asking you, how do you want to die?” The Celestial Thearch gritted her teeth.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

He remembered that Senior White Two had once asked him how he was going to die.

At that time, Song Shuhangs answer was simply a dark history of his life. If he hadn’t been quick-witted at that time and made a contribution in time to atone for his crimes, that answer would have been enough to slice him up by Senior White Two.

Therefore, when faced with the same question again, Song Shuhang had to take it seriously and not answer it casually.

This time, after thinking about it seriously, Song Shuhang tentatively replied, “If I really have to choose a way to die, would I die naturally?”

The Celestial Thearch was speechless.

The white-robed Golden Trigram felt that something was strange. The relationship between the Heavenly Emperor and this Senior Song didn’t seem to be the normal ‘senior and junior’ relationship.

At the very least, from the conversation, it could be seen that the Heavenly Emperor didn’t have any respect for this Senior Song at all. She would threaten to kill him at any time.

This ‘Senior Song was also extremely cowardly. Moreover, his skin was also thick, and he was so cowardly that it came naturally.

“Alright, then you’ll die naturally. I’ll personally go find Senior Song in a few days and make you die of old age,” the Celestial Thearch sneered.

Senior Song, age and die under the influence of the Dao of Time!

“Sorry to disturb you. Goodbye, I won’t contact you again!” Song Shuhang cupped his fists and replied. He felt that the dream was about to end, and it was time to leave Senior Rabbit’s body and return to the Tribulation Transcender Realm.

At that time, his main body would hide in the Netherworld Realm and cultivate properly, not returning to the main world. It would be best if he could open the second sealing pillar that sealed the Scholarly Sage’s ‘Confucian Classics’, and then lock his main body inside.

In this way, even if the Heavenly Emperor came to him, he would not be able to hurt him in a short period of time, since even the ruler of the Netherworld would need 500 years to undo the seal.

“Wonderful, why didn’t I think of this plan before?” Song Shuhang praised himself for his quick-wittedness. As long as he undid the seal of the ‘Confucian Classics’ and filled the favorable impression of the ‘sealing pillar’ to the maximum, it would be equivalent to him having an ‘absolute defensive’ magical treasure!

Unlike the Inner World, which would be sealed by the opponent’s ‘Spatial Imprisonment Technique’ at the critical moment, the fat ball’s ‘Sealing Pillar’ could be opened and closed at any time.

This was simply a life-saving divine skill.

Later on, he would work overtime and use the same method as the Limitless Demon Sect’s Demon Emperor Palace to fill up the sealing pillar in one go!

The Celestial Thearch felt her temples throb.

“Time’s up. I’ve sent you off for a long time, but you’ll have to part ways. Celestial Emperor Fairy, please stay,” Song Shuhang said.

As he spoke, the last stream of the Heavenly Court’s Great Dao flowing light that the Heavenly Emperor had passed down to Gold Trigram fused into his body. At the same time, Song Shuhang also received the last bit of knowledge about the Great Dao of the Heavenly City.

“You can come and go as you please. Senior Song, you’re dreaming,” the

Celestial Thearch stretched out her hand and pointed at the void. The Dao of Time was activated under her control... She wanted to use the laws of time to forcefully leave behind Song Shuhangs ‘future’ consciousness.

After the ancient Heavenly City’s Dao was passed down to Golden Trigram, the Heavenly Emperor lost this ‘Dao of Immortality.’ However, there was another Dao of Time hidden in her body that had transformed and split from the Dao of the ancient Heavenly City.

After losing the Great Dao of the Heavenly City, she temporarily fell to the Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender Realm. However, in just an instant, she quickly switched over and used the ‘Dao of Time’, stepping into the Immortal Realm once again.

She didn’t even lose much of her strength.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

A woman’s heart was like a needle at the bottom of the sea.

Previously, she had told him to scram, but when he really wanted to scram, she forced him to stay.

The power of time wrapped around Golden Trigram’s body and locked onto Song Shuhangs consciousness.

However... Song Shuhangs consciousness didn’t pause for too long.

In just two or three breaths, the dreamland ended, and Song Shuhang’s consciousness disappeared from the white-robed Golden Trigram’s body.

The Celestial Thearch’s finger pointed stiffly in the air.

“He left,” the white-robed Gold Trigram said. At this moment, the aura on his body became thicker and thicker. A faint Emperor Pressure was activated and spread out from his body.

From this moment on, he was the new Heavenly Emperor, Emperor Gold Trigram.

The Celestial Thearch slowly retracted her arm.

“Also, did I come into contact with this Senior Song somewhere? To be precise... Is it possible that in my sealed memories, I was possessed by Senior Song?” Golden Trigram raised his head and looked at the Heavenly Emperor.

After receiving the Dao of the ancient Heavenly City and becoming the new Heavenly Emperor, he felt as if some memory fragments in the depths of his soul were awakening.

This Senior Song seemed to have possessed him before. Previously, Senior Song had also tried to introduce himself to him. So, he had indeed come into contact with this Senior Song before, and it was very likely that the two of them knew each other. Had they known each other since ancient times, before the establishment of the Heavenly City?

The Celestial Thearch didn’t answer Golden Trigram’s question. She just raised her head and remained deep in thought.

A day later, in the void of the Tribulation Transcender.

Song Shuhangs dormant primordial spirit suddenly became active again.

“You’re back? The dream is finally over,” Song Shuhangs primordial spirit sighed.

At the same time, he received a message from the Celestial Thearch in his mind.

It was a message from yesterday.

“Ding Your ‘scoundrel friend’ Heavenly Emperor has sent you a drop of energy from a distance. P.S.: Senior Song, this is today’s energy share In the future, let’s meet again in the ‘ancient time’!”

When Song Shuhang read the second half of the sentence, his heart trembled..

If you lead a blameless life, you won’t fear ghosts knocking at the door in the dead of night. But if guilt lurks within, certain keywords can make your heart race — just like in the case of Song Shuhang.

Celestial Emperor, Ancient Era, Goodbye...This combination of words hit Song Shuhang’s heart.

He stared at the Celestial Thearch’s message for a long time. However, he was not sure if the Celestial Thearch had really guessed his identity or if he was just bluffing.

‘No matter what, I will never admit that I once led the first Heavenly Emperor to jump off a cliff.’ Song Shuhang thought to himself.

If you confess, I’ll be lenient, and you’ll go to jail.

Regardless of whether he was beaten to death or not, he just did not want to admit it.

Just as he was thinking, the Celestial Thearch sent a new message.

[Your ‘scoundrel friend’ Heavenly Emperor has sent you a drop of energy from afar. P.S.: Senior Song, this is the energy share for today Have you woken up from your seclusion?]

“F * ck!” Song Shuhang said.

How did the Celestial Thearch know that he had already woken up from his closed-door cultivation?

Could it be that she is still spying on me?

He hurriedly turned his head and looked around in the void of the Tribulation Transcender Realm, his divine sense covering the surroundings.

However, he could only see Senior White, Fairy Skylark, Senior Seventh

Cultivator of True Virtue, and Senior Spirit Butterfly. The spirit butterfly and

If she really is hiding in the Tribulation Transcender Void to spy on me, she can hide in an area outside the range of my divine sense. The situation is not good for me.” Song Shuhang said in distress.

The virtuous lamia was confused.

Aren’t you in seclusion? When did he offend the Celestial Thearch?

At the same time, he silently organized the knowledge of the Heavenly Court’s

Great Dao in his mind.

The ‘knowledge of the path of the Heavenly City’ was incomparably huge. Song Shuhang had specially drawn a section in his head to store this part of the ‘knowledge of the Heavenly City.

Shuhangs body! It was different from the aura of the Great Dao that Song

Shuhang had gotten from collecting the fragments of the ancient Heavenly City in the past. This time, the aura of the Great Dao of the ancient Heavenly City was emitted by Song Shuhang himself.

Shuhang was in contact with the path of the Heavenly Court?

The virtuous lamia couldn’t help but worry.

She was once a member of the ancient Heavenly City and had a close relationship with the Heavenly City’s destroyer, Cheng Goudan. Therefore, she knew how dangerous the Great Dao of the ancient Heavenly City was.

Once one was infected by this Great Dao, it would be very difficult to escape. If they weren’t careful, they would be bound by the Great Dao of the celestial heavens, and even Immortals wouldn’t be able to easily escape.

“Song the virtuous lamia said, trying to remind Song Shuhang not to come into contact with the path of the Heavenly City.

However, just as she opened her mouth, she discovered that the aura of the ancient Heavenly City on Song Shuhangs body had suddenly disappeared without a trace.

The virtuous lamia was confused.

“What’s wrong, Fairy @#%&?” Song Shuhang asked.

The virtuous lamia rolled her eyes.

“Did I mispronounce your name again?” Song Shuhang understood the meaning of the virtuous lamia’s words. Then, he tried to roll his tongue and struggle to utter a few syllables of the ancient language,

Song Shuhang gave up struggling after a few tries. “By the way, Fairy Virtue, do you want to consider changing your name?”

“Song Goudan!” the virtuous lamia said angrily.

” It’s Cheng Goudan. Father Goudan personally changed my name. We shouldn’t change his words,” Song Shuhang said with a laugh. He was even considering whether or not he should personally bestow the Daoist name ‘Cheng Goudan’ to the ruler of the Netherworld and make it known to the world.

“What the hell?” Fairy Cheng Lin’s voice sounded in the ears of Song Shuhang and the virtuous lamia.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

This was the Tribulation Transcender Void, yet Fairy Cheng Lin could still sense his words?

The virtuous lamia’s voice became cheerful.

“Why didn’t you go into seclusion in the Tribulation Transcender Void? Why did you tag me for no reason?” Fairy Cheng Lin said angrily. She was chatting with Father Goudan when she suddenly sensed someone calling her ‘Cheng Goudan’. Therefore, she didn’t even think about it and directly used the ‘cultivation chat’ function to transfer Song Shuhangs flight route.

After changing the line, she looked around and found that it was indeed Song Shuhang who kept pinging her.

Moreover, she could sense that Song Shuhang was in seclusion while crazily swiping the Saber Nurturing Technique in the air. The QR code on his back was constantly flashing, and there were monkeys singing above his head.

What was this guy trying to do?

“Actually, I just finished my seclusion,” Song Shuhang replied. “How long have you been in seclusion?” Fairy Cheng Lin asked.

“One...One day?” Song Shuhang wasn’t sure of the time.

‘ Promise me that you won’t tarnish the name of ‘closed-door; okay? Also, don’t keep tagging me for no reason,” Fairy Cheng Lin said.

The virtuous lamia said, “Slander, smear.’

Song Shuhang was speechless.

Fairy Cheng Lin and the virtuous lamia were both members of the ancient Heavenly City, so they should know how to build the ‘heavenly palace buildings’, right?

“Speak. ”

“Cheng Gou...Fairy Lin, do you know how to stabilize the palaces of the ancient Heavenly City after they are materialized using the ‘illusory reality?” Song Shuhang asked.

“It’s too dangerous for you to come into contact with the immortal path of the celestial heavens.’

Cheng Lin and she had a tacit understanding. Just as she was about to remind Shuhang about this matter, Cheng Lin reminded him on her behalf.

“Fairy, don’t misunderstand. I don’t have the intention of coming into contact with the path of the ancient Heavenly City...l just want to build a small house in the void of the Tribulation Transcender Realm.” Song Shuhang replied.

Fairy Cheng Lin and the virtuous lamia were confused.

“The main reason I went into seclusion this time was to build a good relationship with the Tribulation Transcender Void and gain a favorable impression of him. I thought about it and felt that building a small home in the Tribulation Transcender Void would be beneficial to cultivating the relationship between me and the Tribulation Transcender Void.” Song Shuhang explained, “Therefore, I thought of the ‘Heavenly Palace Construction’ section of the Path of the Heavenly City. However, I don’t understand the second half of the Heavenly Palace Construction Section.”

“You don’t understand?” Fairy Cheng Lin immediately caught the key word..

“You really came into contact with the Great Dao of the Heavenly Court?”

—Unless the successor of the succession isn’t ‘others’.

You want me to introduce Song Shuhang?

awesome..

His figure crossed the space and reached out to lift Doudou up high. Then, he imitated Senior Yellow Mountain’s tone and said, “Go ahead and advance,

Doudou.’

Doudou was speechless.

The only thing it didn’t want was to be raised high by Shuhang and say such words!

“I’m here, Senior Yellow Mountain,” Song Shuhang said after putting Doudou down.

“Then let’s go.” Venerable Yellow Mountain handed over a piece of paper. I just contacted Dao Monarch Li. He is currently hiding in his cave abode on the moon. These are the coordinates.’

“No problem. We’ll go there directly.” Song Shuhang nodded, and then gently shook the hair on his head... He pretended to be Pavilion Master Chu opening the spatial gateway.

Another portal opened, leading to the moon’s coordinates.

“Senior Yellow Mountain, you go first.” Song Shuhang said. He had to maintain this spatial gate.

Venerable Yellow Mountain didn’t suspect anything. He grabbed a cosmos bag from the table, and after giving instructions to Doudou, he stood up and stepped into the spatial gateway.

The moon. Daolord Li’s hidden estate.

“Yellow Mountain said that he and that senior monk will come to find me directly. I wonder when they will arrive.” Daolord Li organized the items that might be useful for exploring the ruins.

In addition, he also wanted to see the junior fellow daoist of the Yellow Mountain Family who had great merit and had a strong defense.

As he spoke, a Space Gate suddenly opened at the entrance of his cave abode.

The ripples of spiritual energy coming from the spatial gate were extremely strong, and it immediately alerted Daolord Li.

Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender?

Why would a Ninth Stage Tribulation Transcender come looking for me at this time? Was it a random teleportation error? Or did he take a fancy to the information on the ‘special substance’ in my hands and come to ask for it from me?

Instantly, dozens of thoughts appeared in Daolord Li’s mind.

But right after, Venerable Yellow Mountain’s familiar figure stepped out of the spatial gateway.

“Yellow Mountain?” Daolord Li said, stunned.

When you said ‘come directly to me’, did you mean to come directly through the spatial gate?

You almost scared me to death, alright?

“I’m here, Dao Monarch Li. Open the door,” Venerable Yellow Mountain said with a smile.

Daolord Li formed a Dao-seal and opened the door to the hidden immortal’s cave, allowing Yellow Mountain to enter.

After Venerable Yellow Mountain entered, Dao Monarch Li went up to him and gave him a hug. Where is the other fellow daoist?”

He looked at the spatial gate at the entrance of the cave abode. The other fellow daoist Huang Shan mentioned couldn’t be the fellow daoist who opened the spatial gate, right?

As they spoke, the spatial gate flashed, and another figure stepped out.

When this figure appeared, it was accompanied by a sky full of light of virtue. At the same time, seven Sage Names appeared in Daolord Li’s mind.

Ba... Tyrannical Song?

Daolord Li’s entire body stiffened.

Why was this big shot here?

“He f s here. This is the fellow daoist with a very strong defense that I was talking about.” Mother Yellow Mountain waved at Song Shuhang from afar.

I just wanted a meat shield with a strong defense, and you actually pulled Big Boss Tyrannical Song over?

Also...

Yellow Mountain, you look like a docile chap, but you actually know how to scare people.

When did Tyrannical Song become your junior? Have you watched him grow?

Are you the reincarnation of a big shot from ancient times?

Where is your face?

Was he shameless?

Just as he was thinking.

At the entrance of the cave abode, Big Boss Tyrannical Song called out to Venerable Yellow Mountain from afar, “Senior Yellow Mountain, I’m here!”

Yellow Mountain...Senior?

Senior?

Tyrannical Song called Senior Yellow Mountain?

Daolord Li stared blankly at his best friend Yellow Mountain.

F * Ck.... I really didn’t know that you had such a powerful background!

“Great Yellow Mountain, which ancient big shot are you the reincarnation of?” Dao Monarch Li asked, his voice filled with a mixture of awe and resignation. “Tell me, so 1 can pay respects at the grave of your former life.”

Dao Monarch Li stared at Venerable Yellow Mountain with a despondent expression.

Hearing the formidable Tyrannical Song sweetly address Fellow Daoist Yellow Mountain as ‘senior’ made Dao Monarch Li feel like he was on the verge of kneeling.

At that moment, Tyrannical Song was waving his hand as he approached.

Dao Monarch Li was unsure of how to approach Yellow Mountain’s ‘junior! , Tyrannical Song—after all, this was a man who could make the entire universe tremble!

“Don’t be nervous; just treat Shuhang normally—he’s a very easygoing fellow daoist,” Venerable Yellow Mountain advised, his words belying his true feelings. “If you spend too much time with me, though, you’ll need to come to me to buy the secret fruit-flavored ‘quick-acting heart-saving pill.”‘ Dao Monarch Li was speechless.

Just treat him normally? How could he do so in such a situation!

“You stand in my position and face Tyrannical Song. Why don’t you try staying calm?” he challenged.

“But, turning back to our conversation, Dao Monarch Li, have you noticed that someone has been watching your immortal’s cave?” Venerable Yellow Mountain subtly changed the subject.

As Dao Monarch Li opened the door to his estate to welcome his guest, several shadowy figures appeared, lurking in the area.

“They’ve been here for a while, but my cave abode has remained hidden, so they could only monitor this area. Now that the door to my cave abode is open, they will likely gather here silently. They are a bunch of rats, hiding their heads and showing their tails,” Dao Monarch Li said with disdain. Venerable Yellow Mountain smiled and said, “After all, the special substance you have is a treasure that can enhance the spiritual sense of a life-bound magical treasure...” He paused, then added, “How did your information leak out? You’ve been too careless.’

“l was too careless,” Dao Monarch Li admitted, his tone filled with annoyance. “I was too excited after obtaining the treasure and didn’t take any precautions. I tried to use the treasure to upgrade one of my flying swords... and unfortunately, this process was accidentally discovered by someone. This forced me to hide here and there for a few days.”

Excitement often clouded judgment, and Dao Monarch Li, usually so cautious, had made such a low-level mistake.

Across from him...

Song Shuhang had also noticed the group covertly monitoring him. After a moment’s contemplation, he guessed the reason they were watching Dao Monarch Li.

It seemed that quite a few people were eyeing the special substance in Dao Monarch Li’s possession, which could enhance the spiritual sense of magical artifacts.

The cultivation world was indeed a vast jianghu. Where there was a jianghu, a darker side was inevitable.

Respecting Mother Yellow Mountain, he decided to help Dao Monarch Li. After all, the friends of Yellow Mountain’s mother were considered friends of the members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group.

Meanvvhile, the group secretly observing Dao Monarch Li’s immortal’s cave trembled, their legs weakened and their stomachs churned with anxiety.

They had not anticipated that Big Boss Tyrannical Song would appear at this crucial moment.

Initially, they had only intended to learn about a Level 10 Miniboss, but unexpectedly, they encountered a Level 100 million Ultimate Boss alongside the Miniboss.

If not for their robust mental fortitude, they would have collapsed by now.

They hadn’t expected Dao Monarch Li to have any connection with Tyrannical Song.

What was the nature of the relationship between Dao Monarch Li and Tyrannical Song?

If it were merely a one-time cooperation, that would be manageable, Once the partnership between Dao Monarch Li and Tyrannical Song concluded, they could seize an opportunity to strike.

However, if there was a deeper connection between Dao Monarch Li and Tyrannical Song... Well, anyone who harbored intentions against Dao Monarch Li would be courting death.

In the past year, the most prominent figure in the cultivation world was

undoubtedly Tyrannical Song.

Moreover, it was rumored that not long ago, Tyrannical Song had challenged the heavyweights of the universe on Mars. It was reported that more than ten such figures had been decisively defeated by Tyrannical Song!

While the details of the battle were beyond the comprehension of mere juniors like them, they could still catch wind of various rumors.

For instance, it was rumored that Tyrannical Song was developing his own ‘Tyrannical Write’. Additionally, there were whispers that Tyrannical Song might have ascended to the same realm as the Scholarly Sage and Heavenly Emperor.

“Let’s leave before we provoke Senior Tyrannical Song,” they concluded silently. “We’ll retreat quietly, and later, I’ll find a way to discreetly inquire about the relationship between Tyrannical Song and Daoist Li.”

With that thought, the monitoring group began to discreetly withdraw.

However, just then, Big Boss Tyrannical Song unexpectedly called out with a cheerful wave, “Senior Dao Monarch Li, I’m here!”

The members of the monitoring team were left speechless.

Senior?

Dao Monarch Li?

Tyrannical Songs cheerful greeting resonated like a thunderclap from ancient times, reverberating endlessly in the minds of all present.

The surveillance team members, who were poised to retreat, felt as if they were being choked. Their mouths gaped open, and they repeatedly swallowed, though their throats were parched and devoid of saliva.

What was Dao Monarch Li’s true background?

Could he actually be Big Boss Tyrannical Songs senior?

Yet, Dao Monarch Li was only a Sixth Stage True Monarch. How could he possibly be considered a senior to Big Boss Tyrannical Song?

Only one explanation seemed plausible: Dao Monarch Li must be the reincarnation of some ancient, significant figure. Furthermore, he must have shared a close relationship with Tyrannical Song in his previous life, enough to be considered his senior!

This revelation suggested that perhaps the treasure relic capable of enhancing the spiritual sense of a Dharma treasure was a remnant from Dao Monarch Li’s previous life.

With this new understanding, many things began to fall into place.

This revelation was terrifying indeed, and Senior Dao Monarch Li had concealed his true capabilities masterfully, playing the part of a cunning figure who bides his time.

“Retreat quickly,” they urged one another. “Then, immediately relay this information back.”

Unbeknownst to them, Dao Monarch Li stood dumbfounded.

Across from him, Dao Monarch Li, who had been pondering how to interact with Tyrannical Song, froze, his expression vacant.

He had envisioned numerous scenarios for his encounter with Tyrannical Song.

For instance, he might have respectfully greeted Tyrannical Song with a bow, saying, “Senior Tyrannical Song, welcome to my residence.” He could have added that Tyrannical Songs presence brightened his cave abode.

Alternatively, under Yellow Mountain’s endorsement, perhaps Big Boss Tyrannical Song would have humbled himself to acknowledge a peer, graciously addressing him as ‘Fellow Daoist Li t . Such an interaction would have provided ample material for Dao Monarch Li to boast about for years to come.

‘Big Boss Tyrannical Song once spoke to me as an equal and called me fellow daoist’—such a statement would have been a source of pride for years.

However, Tyrannical Songs unexpected address of ‘Senior Dao Monarch Li t in front of a crowd had completely disrupted Dao Monarch Li’s calculations.

He turned his head and gazed at Mount Huang, pondering, “Could it be that, like Huang Shan, I am the reincarnation of some ancient luminary?”
